{

    while ((c = getchar()) == ' ' || c == '\t') // skip white spaces
        ;

    {
        return c; // not a number
    }

    int sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;
    if (c == '-')
    {
        c = getchar();
        if (!isdigit(c) && c != '.')
        {
            ungetc(c, stdin);
            return '-';
        }
    }

    int number = 0;
    if (isdigit(c))
    {
        do {
            number = number * 10 + (c - '0');
            c = getchar();
        } while (isdigit(c));
    }

    if (c == '.')
    {
        c = getchar();
        double fraction = 1.0;
        while (isdigit(c))
        {
            number = number * 10 + (c - '0');
            fraction *= 10;
            c = getchar();
        }
        number = sign * number / fraction;
    }

    if (c != EOF)
    {
        ungetc(c, stdin);
    }

    return number;
}

int getop(char *s)
{
    int c;
    // skip whitespace
    while ((*s = c = getchar()) == ' ' || c == '\t')
        ;
    
    *(s+1) = '\0';
    
    if (!isdigit(c) && c != '.')
        return c; // not a number
    
    if (isdigit(c)) // collect integer part
        while (isdigit(*++s = c = getchar()))
            ;
    
    if (c == '.') // collect fraction part
        while (isdigit(*++s = c = getchar()))
            ;

    return NUMBER;
}

int getop(char *s)
                'next token or line'
                Complete the 'next token or line' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'next token or line'. 
                
Time taken: 3.046257495880127 seconds
Received response: int getop(char *s) {
  int i = 0;
  char c;

  // Skipping any leading white spaces
  while (isspace(s[i])) {
    i++;
  }

  c = s[i];

  // Check if the token is a number
  if (isdigit(c) || c == '.') {
    // Code for parsing a number
    while (isdigit(s[i]) || s[i] == '.') {
      i++;
    }
    return NUMBER_TOKEN;
  }
  
  // Check if the token is an operator
  else if (c == '+' || c == '-' || c == '*' || c == '/') {
    // Code for parsing an operator
    return OPERATOR_TOKEN;
  }
  
  // Check if the token is a newline character
  else if (c == '\n') {
    return NEWLINE_TOKEN;
  }
  
  // If the token is none of the above, return an error code
  else {
    return ERROR_TOKEN;
